<div class="bg-card flex min-h-0 flex-1 flex-col overflow-hidden border-default shadow-big mx-auto rounded-t-2xl border-[0.5px] @min-[750px]:max-w-[750px] @min-[750px]:min-w-[min(750px,100%)]"><div class="flex min-h-0 min-w-0 flex-1"><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden h-full w-full" style="position: relative; --radix-scroll-area-corner-width: 0px; --radix-scroll-area-corner-height: 0px;"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit] [&amp;&gt;div]:!block" style="overflow: hidden scroll;"><div style="min-width: 100%; display: table;"><div class="h-full w-full"><div contenteditable="true" translate="no" class="tiptap ProseMirror canva-editor markdown-editor markdown-container-style min-h-full flex-1" tabindex="0"><h1><strong>Unix Domain Sockets (AF_UNIX): Локальные сокеты для межпроцессового взаимодействия</strong></h1><hr contenteditable="false"><h2><strong>Введение</strong></h2><p><strong>Unix Domain Sockets (UDS)</strong> — это механизм межпроцессового взаимодействия (IPC), который позволяет процессам обмениваться данными через <strong>локальные сокеты</strong>, аналогично сетевым сокетам (<code>AF_INET</code>), но <strong>без использования сетевого стека</strong>. В отличие от сетевых сокетов, UDS работают <strong>только в пределах одной машины</strong> и используют <strong>файловую систему</strong> для идентификации сокетов.</p><h3><strong>Ключевые особенности Unix Domain Sockets:</strong></h3><table style="min-width: 50px"><colgroup><col style="min-width: 25px"><col style="min-width: 25px"></colgroup><tbody><tr><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Особенность</strong></p></th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Описание</strong></p></th></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Локальность</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Работают только между процессами на <strong>одной машине</strong>.</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Высокая производительность</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Нет оверхеда на сетевой стек (TCP/IP), что делает их <strong>быстрее сетевых сокетов</strong>.</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Идентификация</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Сокеты представляются как <strong>файлы в файловой системе</strong> (обычно в <code>/tmp/</code> или <code>/var/run/</code>).</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Типы сокетов</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Поддерживают <strong>потоковые сокеты (SOCK_STREAM)</strong> и <strong>датаграммные сокеты (SOCK_DGRAM)</strong>.</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Безопасность</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Права доступа к сокету определяются <strong>правами на файл</strong> в файловой системе.</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Поддержка в Linux</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Полная поддержка в ядре Linux.</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Совместимость</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Поддерживаются во всех Unix-подобных системах (Linux, macOS, BSD и т. д.).</p></td></tr></tbody></table><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>Когда использовать Unix Domain Sockets?</strong></h3><p>✅ <strong>Используйте UDS, если:</strong></p><ul><li><p>Вам нужен <strong>быстрый обмен данными между процессами на одной машине</strong>.</p></li><li><p>Вы хотите использовать <strong>знакомый API сокетов</strong> (аналогично сетевым сокетам).</p></li><li><p>Вам нужна <strong>поддержка потокового (SOCK_STREAM) или датаграммного (SOCK_DGRAM) обмена</strong>.</p></li><li><p>Вы хотите <strong>изолировать процессы</strong> (например, для микросервисов или модулей программы).</p></li></ul><p>❌ <strong>Не используйте UDS, если:</strong></p><ul><li><p>Вам нужен <strong>обмен данными между разными машинами</strong> (используйте сетевые сокеты <code>AF_INET</code>).</p></li><li><p>Вам нужна <strong>максимальная производительность</strong> (используйте разделяемую память).</p></li><li><p>Вы передаёте <strong>очень большие объёмы данных</strong> (UDS имеют ограничения на размер сообщений).</p></li></ul><hr contenteditable="false"><hr contenteditable="false"><h2><strong>1. Теоретические основы Unix Domain Sockets</strong></h2><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>1.1. Что такое Unix Domain Socket?</strong></h3><p>Unix Domain Socket — это <strong>конечная точка связи</strong>, которая позволяет процессам обмениваться данными через <strong>ядро операционной системы</strong>. В отличие от сетевых сокетов, UDS не используют сетевые протоколы (например, TCP/IP), а работают <strong>непосредственно через ядро</strong>.</p><h4><strong>Типы Unix Domain Sockets:</strong></h4><table style="min-width: 100px"><colgroup><col style="min-width: 25px"><col style="min-width: 25px"><col style="min-width: 25px"><col style="min-width: 25px"></colgroup><tbody><tr><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Тип</strong></p></th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Описание</strong></p></th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Аналог в сетевых сокетах</strong></p></th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Пример использования</strong></p></th></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>SOCK_STREAM</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Потоковый сокет (надёжная передача данных с гарантией порядка).</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>TCP</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Обмен структурированными данными (например, JSON, протоколы типа HTTP).</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>SOCK_DGRAM</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Датаграммный сокет (ненадёжная передача данных без гарантии порядка).</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>UDP</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Передача небольших сообщений (например, логи или уведомления).</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>SOCK_SEQPACKET</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Последовательный пакетный сокет (надёжная передача сообщений с сохранением границ).</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>SCTP</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Передача сообщений с чёткими границами (например, протоколы на основе сообщений).</p></td></tr></tbody></table><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>1.2. Как работают Unix Domain Sockets?</strong></h3><ol><li><p><strong>Создание сокета</strong>:</p><ul><li><p>Сервер создаёт сокет с помощью <code>socket(AF_UNIX, SOCK_STREAM, 0)</code>.</p></li><li><p>Сервер связывает сокет с <strong>файлом в файловой системе</strong> с помощью <code>bind()</code>.</p></li><li><p>Сервер начинает прослушивание входящих соединений с помощью <code>listen()</code>.</p></li><li><p>Сервер принимает соединения с помощью <code>accept()</code>.</p></li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Подключение клиента</strong>:</p><ul><li><p>Клиент создаёт сокет с помощью <code>socket(AF_UNIX, SOCK_STREAM, 0)</code>.</p></li><li><p>Клиент подключается к серверу с помощью <code>connect()</code>, указывая путь к файлу сокета.</p></li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Обмен данными</strong>:</p><ul><li><p>Сервер и клиент обмениваются данными с помощью <code>send()</code>/<code>recv()</code> (для <code>SOCK_STREAM</code>) или <code>sendto()</code>/<code>recvfrom()</code> (для <code>SOCK_DGRAM</code>).</p></li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Закрытие соединения</strong>:</p><ul><li><p>Сервер и клиент закрывают сокеты с помощью <code>close()</code>.</p></li><li><p>Файл сокета удаляется из файловой системы с помощью <code>unlink()</code>.</p></li></ul></li></ol><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>1.3. Преимущества и недостатки Unix Domain Sockets</strong></h3><table style="min-width: 50px"><colgroup><col style="min-width: 25px"><col style="min-width: 25px"></colgroup><tbody><tr><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Преимущества</strong></p></th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Недостатки</strong></p></th></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>✅ <strong>Высокая производительность</strong> (нет оверхеда на сетевой стек).</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>❌ <strong>Работают только на одной машине</strong> (не подходят для распределённых систем).</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>✅ <strong>Простой и знакомый API</strong> (аналогично сетевым сокетам).</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>❌ <strong>Ограничения на размер сообщений</strong> (зависят от реализации ядра).</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>✅ <strong>Поддержка потокового и датаграммного обмена</strong>.</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>❌ <strong>Требуется синхронизация</strong> для работы с несколькими клиентами.</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>✅ <strong>Безопасность</strong> (права доступа определяются файловой системой).</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>❌ <strong>Сложность отладки</strong> (ошибки могут быть связаны с правами на файл сокета).</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>✅ <strong>Поддержка в стандартной библиотеке</strong> (нет необходимости в дополнительных зависимостях).</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>❌ <strong>Не подходят для передачи больших файлов</strong> (используйте разделяемую память).</p></td></tr></tbody></table><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>1.4. Сравнение с другими механизмами IPC</strong></h3><table style="min-width: 150px"><colgroup><col style="min-width: 25px"><col style="min-width: 25px"><col style="min-width: 25px"><col style="min-width: 25px"><col style="min-width: 25px"><col style="min-width: 25px"></colgroup><tbody><tr><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Механизм IPC</strong></p></th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Unix Domain Sockets</strong></p></th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Разделяемая память</strong></p></th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Очереди сообщений</strong></p></th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Каналы (Pipe/FIFO)</strong></p></th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Сетевые сокеты (AF_INET)</strong></p></th></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Скорость</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>⭐⭐⭐⭐ (очень высокая)</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐ (максимальная)</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>⭐⭐⭐ (средняя)</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>⭐⭐ (низкая)</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>⭐⭐ (низкая, из-за сетевого стека)</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Тип обмена</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Потоковый/датаграммный</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Память</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Сообщения</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Поток байтов</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Поток байтов</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Локальность</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Локальные (одна машина)</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Локальные</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Локальные</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Локальные</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Сетевые (между машинами)</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Синхронизация</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Требуется вручную</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Требуется вручную</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Встроенная</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Нет</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Требуется вручную</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Сложность</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Средняя</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Высокая</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Низкая</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Низкая</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Средняя</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Поддержка в Linux</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Да</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Да</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Да</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Да</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Да</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Переносимость</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Unix-подобные системы</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Unix-подобные системы</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Unix-подобные системы</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>POSIX</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Все системы</p></td></tr></tbody></table><hr contenteditable="false"><hr contenteditable="false"><h2><strong>2. Основы работы с Unix Domain Sockets</strong></h2><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>2.1. Основные функции для работы с UDS</strong></h3><table style="min-width: 75px"><colgroup><col style="min-width: 25px"><col style="min-width: 25px"><col style="min-width: 25px"></colgroup><tbody><tr><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Функция</strong></p></th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Описание</strong></p></th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Аналог в сетевых сокетах</strong></p></th></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>socket(AF_UNIX, type, 0)</code></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Создаёт Unix Domain Socket.</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>socket(AF_INET, type, 0)</code></p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>bind()</code></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Связывает сокет с файлом в файловой системе.</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>bind()</code></p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>listen()</code></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Переводит сокет в режим прослушивания.</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>listen()</code></p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>accept()</code></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Принимает входящее соединение.</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>accept()</code></p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>connect()</code></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Подключается к серверному сокету.</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>connect()</code></p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>send()</code>/<code>recv()</code></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Отправка/получение данных (для <code>SOCK_STREAM</code>).</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>send()</code>/<code>recv()</code></p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>sendto()</code>/<code>recvfrom()</code></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Отправка/получение данных (для <code>SOCK_DGRAM</code>).</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>sendto()</code>/<code>recvfrom()</code></p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>close()</code></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Закрывает сокет.</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>close()</code></p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>unlink()</code></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Удаляет файл сокета из файловой системы.</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>—</p></td></tr></tbody></table><hr contenteditable="false"><h3>**2.2. Структура <code>sockaddr_un**</code></h3><p>Для работы с Unix Domain Sockets используется структура <code>sockaddr_un</code>, которая определяет <strong>адрес сокета</strong> (путь к файлу в файловой системе).</p><div class="react-renderer node-codeBlock"><pre as="pre" spellcheck="false" class="code-block-wrapper group/codeblock" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div transition-colors focus-visible:ring-default focus-visible:ring-offset-1 aria-disabled:text-hint aria-disabled:cursor-not-allowed aria-busy:cursor-wait aria-busy:text-transparent aria-disabled:aria-busy:text-transparent bg-state-ghost text-default hover:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-hover active:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-press gap-1 text-xs p-0 rounded-md size-6"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy size-3.5" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div><code><div data-node-view-content="" style="white-space: pre-wrap;"><div data-node-view-content-react="" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: inherit;"><span class="hljs-class hljs-keyword">struct</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">sockaddr_un</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">addr</span><span class="hljs-class">;</span>
<span class="hljs-built_in">memset</span>(&amp;addr, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(addr));
addr.sun_family = AF_UNIX;
<span class="hljs-built_in">strncpy</span>(addr.sun_path, <span class="hljs-string">"/tmp/my_socket"</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(addr.sun_path) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>);</div></div></code></pre></div><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>2.3. Типы Unix Domain Sockets</strong></h3><h4><strong>1. Потоковые сокеты (<code>SOCK_STREAM</code>)</strong></h4><ul><li><p><strong>Надёжная передача данных</strong> (гарантируется порядок и доставка).</p></li><li><p><strong>Аналог TCP</strong> в сетевых сокетах.</p></li><li><p><strong>Используются для:</strong></p><ul><li><p>Обмена структурированными данными (например, JSON, XML).</p></li><li><p>Реализации протоколов типа HTTP или gRPC (для локальных вызовов).</p></li></ul></li></ul><h4><strong>2. Датаграммные сокеты (<code>SOCK_DGRAM</code>)</strong></h4><ul><li><p><strong>Ненадёжная передача данных</strong> (нет гарантии порядка или доставки).</p></li><li><p><strong>Аналог UDP</strong> в сетевых сокетах.</p></li><li><p><strong>Используются для:</strong></p><ul><li><p>Передачи небольших сообщений (например, логов или уведомлений).</p></li><li><p>Реализации простых протоколов обмена сообщениями.</p></li></ul></li></ul><h4><strong>3. Последовательные пакетные сокеты (<code>SOCK_SEQPACKET</code>)</strong></h4><ul><li><p><strong>Надёжная передача сообщений</strong> с сохранением границ.</p></li><li><p><strong>Аналог SCTP</strong> в сетевых сокетах.</p></li><li><p><strong>Используются для:</strong></p><ul><li><p>Передачи сообщений с чёткими границами (например, протоколы на основе сообщений).</p></li></ul></li></ul><hr contenteditable="false"><hr contenteditable="false"><h2><strong>3. Потоковые сокеты (SOCK_STREAM)</strong></h2><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>3.1. Пример сервера на потоковых сокетах</strong></h3><p>Сервер создаёт сокет, связывает его с файлом, прослушивает входящие соединения и принимает клиентов.</p><h4>**Код сервера: <code>unix_stream_server_c_1.txt**</code></h4><div class="react-renderer node-codeBlock"><pre as="pre" spellcheck="false" class="code-block-wrapper group/codeblock" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div class="absolute top-2 right-2 z-1 flex items-center gap-0.5 transition-opacity select-none opacity-0 group-hover/codeblock:opacity-100" contenteditable="false"><button type="button" class="flex items-center justify-center text-center font-medium cursor-pointer outline-hidden focus-visible:ring-3 relative whitespace-nowrap aria-haspopup="dialog" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="radix-_r_kc_" data-state="closed">C<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down ms-1 size-3 opacity-50" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button><button type="button" class="flex items-center justify-center text-center font-medium cursor-pointer outline-hidden focus-visible:ring-3 relative whitespace-nowrap xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy size-3.5" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div><code><div data-node-view-content="" style="white-space: pre-wrap;"><div data-node-view-content-react="" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: inherit;"><span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/socket.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/un.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;stdio.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;stdlib.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;unistd.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;string.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;errno.h&gt;</span>

<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">define</span><span class="hljs-meta"> SOCKET_PATH </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">"/tmp/unix_stream_socket"</span>

<span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">main</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> server_fd, client_fd;
    <span class="hljs-class hljs-keyword">struct</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">sockaddr_un</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">server_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">, </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">client_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">;</span>
    <span class="hljs-type">socklen_t</span> client_len;
    <span class="hljs-type">char</span> buffer[<span class="hljs-number">256</span>];
    <span class="hljs-type">ssize_t</span> bytes_read;

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Создаём сокет</span>
    server_fd = socket(AF_UNIX, SOCK_STREAM, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (server_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"socket"</span>);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Удаляем файл сокета, если он уже существует</span>
    unlink(SOCKET_PATH);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Инициализируем адрес сервера</span>
    <span class="hljs-built_in">memset</span>(&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr));
    server_addr.sun_family = AF_UNIX;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">strncpy</span>(server_addr.sun_path, SOCKET_PATH, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr.sun_path) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Связываем сокет с файлом</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bind(server_fd, (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr)) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"bind"</span>);
        close(server_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Переводим сокет в режим прослушивания</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (listen(server_fd, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"listen"</span>);
        close(server_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Server: Waiting for connections...\n"</span>);

    <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> (<span class="hljs-number">1</span>) {
        <span class="hljs-comment">// Принимаем входящее соединение</span>
        client_len = <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(client_addr);
        client_fd = accept(server_fd, (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;client_addr, &amp;client_len);
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"accept"</span>);
            <span class="hljs-keyword">continue</span>;
        }

        <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Server: Client connected\n"</span>);

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Читаем данные от клиента</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> ((bytes_read = recv(client_fd, buffer, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(buffer) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>)) &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
            buffer[bytes_read] = <span class="hljs-string">'\0'</span>;
            <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Server: Received: %s\n"</span>, buffer);

            <span class="hljs-comment">// Отправляем ответ клиенту</span>
            <span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">char</span> *response = <span class="hljs-string">"Message received by server!"</span>;
            <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (send(client_fd, response, <span class="hljs-built_in">strlen</span>(response), <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
                perror(<span class="hljs-string">"send"</span>);
                <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
            }
        }

        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bytes_read == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"recv"</span>);
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Закрываем соединение с клиентом</span>
        close(client_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Server: Client disconnected\n"</span>);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Закрываем серверный сокет и удаляем файл</span>
    close(server_fd);
    unlink(SOCKET_PATH);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
}</div></div></code></pre></div><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>3.2. Пример клиента на потоковых сокетах</strong></h3><p>Клиент подключается к серверу, отправляет сообщение и получает ответ.</p><h4>**Код клиента: <code>unix_stream_client_c_1.txt**</code></h4><div <span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">main</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {

    <span class="hljs-class hljs-keyword">struct</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">sockaddr_un</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">server_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">;</span>

    client_fd = socket(AF_UNIX, SOCK_STREAM, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"socket"</span>);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Инициализируем адрес сервера</span>
    <span class="hljs-built_in">memset</span>(&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr));
    server_addr.sun_family = AF_UNIX;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">strncpy</span>(server_addr.sun_path, SOCKET_PATH, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr.sun_path) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Подключаемся к серверу</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (connect(client_fd, (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr)) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"connect"</span>);
        close(client_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Client: Connected to server\n"</span>);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Отправляем сообщение серверу</span>
    <span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">char</span> *message = <span class="hljs-string">"Hello from client!"</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (send(client_fd, message, <span class="hljs-built_in">strlen</span>(message), <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"send"</span>);
        close(client_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Client: Sent: %s\n"</span>, message);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Получаем ответ от сервера</span>
    bytes_read = recv(client_fd, buffer, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(buffer) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bytes_read == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"recv"</span>);
        close(client_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    buffer[bytes_read] = <span class="hljs-string">'\0'</span>;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Client: Received: %s\n"</span>, buffer);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Закрываем соединение</span>
    close(client_fd);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
}</div></div></code></pre></div><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>3.3. xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide ./unix_stream_client</div></div></code></pre></div></li><li><p>Убедитесь, что сервер получил сообщение от клиента и отправил ответ.</p></li></ol><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>3.4. Обработка нескольких клиентов (мультиплексирование)</strong></h3><p>Для обработки нескольких клиентов одновременно можно использовать:</p><ul><li><p><strong>Многопоточность</strong> (один поток на клиента).</p></li><li><p><code>**select()</code>/<code>poll()**</code> для мультиплексирования ввода-вывода.</p></li></ul><h4>**Пример сервера с <code>select()</code>: <code>unix_stream_server_select_c_1.txt**</code></h4><div class="react-renderer node-codeBlock"><pre as="pre" spellcheck="false" class="code-block-wrapper group/codeblock" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div class="absolute top-2 right-2 z-1 flex items-center gap-0.5 transition-opacity select-none opacity-0 group-hover/codeblock:opacity-100" contenteditable="false"><button type="button" class="flex items-center justify-center text-center font-medium cursor-pointer outline-hidden focus-visible:ring-3 relative whitespace-nowrap transition-colors focus-visible:ring-default focus-visible:ring-offset-1 aria-disabled:text-hint aria-disabled:cursor-not-allowed aria-busy:cursor-wait aria-busy:text-transparent aria-disabled:aria-busy:text-transparent bg-state-ghost text-default hover:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-hover active:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-press h-6 gap-1 px-1.5 text-xs rounded-md" aria-haspopup="dialog" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="radix-_r_lm_" data-state="closed">C<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down ms-1 size-3 opacity-50" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button><button type="button" class="flex items-center justify-center text-center font-medium cursor-pointer outline-hidden focus-visible:ring-3 relative whitespace-nowrap transition-colors focus-visible:ring-default focus-visible:ring-offset-1 aria-disabled:text-hint aria-disabled:cursor-not-allowed aria-busy:cursor-wait aria-busy:text-transparent aria-disabled:aria-busy:text-transparent bg-state-ghost text-default hover:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-hover active:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-press gap-1 text-xs p-0 rounded-md size-6"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy size-3.5" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div><code><div data-node-view-content="" style="white-space: pre-wrap;"><div data-node-view-content-react="" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: inherit;"><span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/socket.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/un.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/select.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;stdio.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;stdlib.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;unistd.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;string.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;errno.h&gt;</span>

<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">define</span><span class="hljs-meta"> SOCKET_PATH </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">"/tmp/unix_stream_socket_select"</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">define</span><span class="hljs-meta"> MAX_CLIENTS 10</span>

<span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">main</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> server_fd, client_fds[MAX_CLIENTS];
    <span class="hljs-class hljs-keyword">struct</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">sockaddr_un</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">server_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">;</span>
    fd_set read_fds, master_fds;
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> max_fd = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
    <span class="hljs-type">char</span> buffer[<span class="hljs-number">256</span>];
    <span class="hljs-type">ssize_t</span> bytes_read;

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Инициализируем массив дескрипторов клиентов</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (<span class="hljs-type">int</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; MAX_CLIENTS; i++) {
        client_fds[i] = <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>;
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Создаём сокет</span>
    server_fd = socket(AF_UNIX, SOCK_STREAM, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (server_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"socket"</span>);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Удаляем файл сокета, если он уже существует</span>
    unlink(SOCKET_PATH);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Инициализируем адрес сервера</span>
    <span class="hljs-built_in">memset</span>(&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr));
    server_addr.sun_family = AF_UNIX;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">strncpy</span>(server_addr.sun_path, SOCKET_PATH, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr.sun_path) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Связываем сокет с файлом</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bind(server_fd, (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr)) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"bind"</span>);
        close(server_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Переводим сокет в режим прослушивания</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (listen(server_fd, MAX_CLIENTS) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"listen"</span>);
        close(server_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Инициализируем master_fds</span>
    FD_ZERO(&amp;master_fds);
    FD_SET(server_fd, &amp;master_fds);
    max_fd = server_fd;

    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Server: Waiting for connections...\n"</span>);

    <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> (<span class="hljs-number">1</span>) {
        <span class="hljs-comment">// Копируем master_fds в read_fds</span>
        read_fds = master_fds;

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Ждём активности на любом из дескрипторов</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (select(max_fd + <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, &amp;read_fds, <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>, <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>, <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"select"</span>);
            <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Проверяем серверный сокет на новые соединения</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (FD_ISSET(server_fd, &amp;read_fds)) {
            <span class="hljs-class hljs-keyword">struct</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">sockaddr_un</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">client_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">;</span>
            <span class="hljs-type">socklen_t</span> client_len = <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(client_addr);
            <span class="hljs-type">int</span> client_fd = accept(server_fd, (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;client_addr, &amp;client_len);
            <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
                perror(<span class="hljs-string">"accept"</span>);
            } <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
                <span class="hljs-comment">// Добавляем нового клиента в master_fds</span>
                <span class="hljs-type">int</span> i;
                <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; MAX_CLIENTS; i++) {
                    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fds[i] == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
                        client_fds[i] = client_fd;
                        <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
                    }
                }
                <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (i == MAX_CLIENTS) {
                    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Server: Too many clients\n"</span>);
                    close(client_fd);
                } <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
                    FD_SET(client_fd, &amp;master_fds);
                    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fd &gt; max_fd) {
                        max_fd = client_fd;
                    }
                    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Server: New client connected (fd=%d)\n"</span>, client_fd);
                }
            }
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Проверяем клиентские сокеты на данные</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (<span class="hljs-type">int</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; MAX_CLIENTS; i++) {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fds[i] != <span class="hljs-number">-1</span> &amp;&amp; FD_ISSET(client_fds[i], &amp;read_fds)) {
                bytes_read = recv(client_fds[i], buffer, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(buffer) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
                <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bytes_read &lt;= <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
                    <span class="hljs-comment">// Клиент отключился</span>
                    close(client_fds[i]);
                    FD_CLR(client_fds[i], &amp;master_fds);
                    client_fds[i] = <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>;
                    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Server: Client disconnected (fd=%d)\n"</span>, client_fds[i]);
                } <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
                    buffer[bytes_read] = <span class="hljs-string">'\0'</span>;
                    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Server: Received from client %d: %s\n"</span>, client_fds[i], buffer);

                    <span class="hljs-comment">// Отправляем ответ клиенту</span>
                    <span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">char</span> *response = <span class="hljs-string">"Message received by server!"</span>;
                    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (send(client_fds[i], response, <span class="hljs-built_in">strlen</span>(response), <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
                        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"send"</span>);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Закрываем все сокеты и удаляем файл</span>
    close(server_fd);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (<span class="hljs-type">int</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; MAX_CLIENTS; i++) {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fds[i] != <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
            close(client_fds[i]);
        }
    }
    unlink(SOCKET_PATH);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
}</div></div></code></pre></div><hr contenteditable="false"><hr contenteditable="false"><h2><strong>4. Датаграммные сокеты (SOCK_DGRAM)</strong></h2><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>4.1. Пример сервера на датаграммных сокетах</strong></h3><p>Сервер создаёт сокет, связывает его с файлом и принимает датаграммы от клиентов.</p><h4>**Код сервера: <code>unix_dgram_server_c_1.txt**</code></h4><div class="react-renderer node-codeBlock"><pre as="pre" spellcheck="false" class="code-block-wrapper group/codeblock" data-node-view-wrapper="" class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/socket.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/un.h&gt;</span>

<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;string.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;errno.h&gt;</span>

<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">define</span><span class="hljs-meta"> SOCKET_PATH </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">"/tmp/unix_dgram_socket"</span>

<span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">main</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> server_fd;
    <span class="hljs-class hljs-keyword">struct</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">sockaddr_un</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">server_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">, </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">client_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">;</span>
    <span class="hljs-type">socklen_t</span> client_len;
    <span class="hljs-type">char</span> buffer[<span class="hljs-number">256</span>];
    <span class="hljs-type">ssize_t</span> bytes_read;

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Создаём сокет</span>
    server_fd = socket(AF_UNIX, SOCK_DGRAM, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (server_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"socket"</span>);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Удаляем файл сокета, если он уже существует</span>
    unlink(SOCKET_PATH);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Инициализируем адрес сервера</span>
    <span class="hljs-built_in">memset</span>(&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr));
    server_addr.sun_family = AF_UNIX;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">strncpy</span>(server_addr.sun_path, SOCKET_PATH, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr.sun_path) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Связываем сокет с файлом</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bind(server_fd, (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr)) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"bind"</span>);
        close(server_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Server: Waiting for datagrams...\n"</span>);

    <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> (<span class="hljs-number">1</span>) {
        <span class="hljs-comment">// Получаем датаграмму от клиента</span>
        client_len = <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(client_addr);
        bytes_read = recvfrom(server_fd, buffer, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(buffer) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>,
                              (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;client_addr, &amp;client_len);
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bytes_read == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"recvfrom"</span>);
            <span class="hljs-keyword">continue</span>;
        }

        buffer[bytes_read] = <span class="hljs-string">'\0'</span>;
        <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Server: Received: %s\n"</span>, buffer);

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Отправляем ответ клиенту</span>
        <span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">char</span> *response = <span class="hljs-string">"Datagram received by server!"</span>;
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (sendto(server_fd, response, <span class="hljs-built_in">strlen</span>(response), <span class="hljs-number">0</span>,
                   (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;client_addr, client_len) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"sendto"</span>);
        }
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Закрываем сокет и удаляем файл</span>
    close(server_fd);
    unlink(SOCKET_PATH);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
}</div></div></code></pre></div><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>4.2. Пример клиента на датаграммных сокетах</strong></h3><p>Клиент отправляет датаграмму серверу и получает ответ.</p><h4>**Код клиента: <code>unix_dgram_client_c_1.txt**</code></h4><div <span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/un.h&gt;</span>

<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">define</span><span class="hljs-meta"> SOCKET_PATH </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">"/tmp/unix_dgram_socket"</span>

<span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">main</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> client_fd;
    <span class="hljs-class hljs-keyword">struct</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">sockaddr_un</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">server_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">;</span>

        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"socket"</span>);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Инициализируем адрес сервера</span>
    <span class="hljs-built_in">memset</span>(&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr));
    server_addr.sun_family = AF_UNIX;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">strncpy</span>(server_addr.sun_path, SOCKET_PATH, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr.sun_path) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Отправляем датаграмму серверу</span>
    <span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">char</span> *message = <span class="hljs-string">"Hello from datagram client!"</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (sendto(client_fd, message, <span class="hljs-built_in">strlen</span>(message), <span class="hljs-number">0</span>,
               (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr)) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {

        close(client_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Получаем ответ от сервера</span>
    bytes_read = recvfrom(client_fd, buffer, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(buffer) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>, <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bytes_read == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"recvfrom"</span>);
        close(client_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    buffer[bytes_read] = <span class="hljs-string">'\0'</span>;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Client: Received: %s\n"</span>, buffer);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Закрываем сокет</span>
    close(client_fd);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;

xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide 2"></path></svg></button></div><code><div data-node-view-content="" style="white-space: pre-wrap;"><div data-node-view-content-react="" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: inherit;"><span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/socket.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/un.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;stdio.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;stdlib.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;unistd.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;string.h&gt;</span>

<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">define</span><span class="hljs-meta"> SOCKET_PATH </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">"/tmp/unix_seqpacket_socket"</span>

<span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">main</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> server_fd, client_fd;
    <span class="hljs-class hljs-keyword">struct</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">sockaddr_un</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">server_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">, </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">client_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">;</span>

    server_fd = socket(AF_UNIX, SOCK_SEQPACKET, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (server_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"socket"</span>);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Удаляем файл сокета, если он уже существует</span>
    unlink(SOCKET_PATH);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Инициализируем адрес сервера</span>
    <span class="hljs-built_in">memset</span>(&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr));
    server_addr.sun_family = AF_UNIX;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">strncpy</span>(server_addr.sun_path, SOCKET_PATH, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr.sun_path) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Связываем сокет с файлом</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bind(server_fd, (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr)) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"bind"</span>);
        close(server_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Переводим сокет в режим прослушивания</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (listen(server_fd, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"listen"</span>);
        close(server_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Server: Waiting for connections...\n"</span>);

    <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> (<span class="hljs-number">1</span>) {
        <span class="hljs-comment">// Принимаем входящее соединение</span>
        client_len = <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(client_addr);
        client_fd = accept(server_fd, (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;client_addr, &amp;client_len);
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"accept"</span>);
            <span class="hljs-keyword">continue</span>;
        }

        <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Server: Client connected\n"</span>);

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Читаем пакеты от клиента</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> ((bytes_read = recv(client_fd, buffer, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(buffer) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>)) &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
            buffer[bytes_read] = <span class="hljs-string">'\0'</span>;
            <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Server: Received packet: %s\n"</span>, buffer);

            <span class="hljs-comment">// Отправляем ответ клиенту</span>
            <span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">char</span> *response = <span class="hljs-string">"Packet received by server!"</span>;
            <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (send(client_fd, response, <span class="hljs-built_in">strlen</span>(response), <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
                perror(<span class="hljs-string">"send"</span>);
                <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
            }
        }

        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bytes_read == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"recv"</span>);
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Закрываем соединение с клиентом</span>
        close(client_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Server: Client disconnected\n"</span>);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Закрываем серверный сокет и удаляем файл</span>
    close(server_fd);
    unlink(SOCKET_PATH);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
}</div></div></code></pre></div><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>5.2. Пример клиента на последовательных пакетных сокетах</strong></h3><p>Клиент подключается к серверу, отправляет пакет и получает ответ.</p><h4>**Код клиента:         perror(<span class="hljs-string">"socket"</span>);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Инициализируем адрес сервера</span>

    <span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">char</span> *message = <span class="hljs-string">"Hello from seqpacket client!"</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (send(client_fd, message, <span class="hljs-built_in">strlen</span>(message), <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"send"</span>);

        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Получаем ответ от сервера</span>
    bytes_read = recv(client_fd, buffer, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(buffer) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bytes_read == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"recv"</span>);

        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);

    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Client: Received: %s\n"</span>, buffer);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Закрываем соединение</span>
    close(client_fd);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
}</div></div></code></pre></div><hr contenteditable="false"><hr contenteditable="false"><h2><strong>6. Практические примеры использования</strong></h2><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>6.1. Реализация простого чата на потоковых сокетах</strong></h3><p>В этом примере сервер обрабатывает несколько клиентов, и каждый клиент может отправлять сообщения, которые сервер рассылает всем подключённым клиентам.</p><h4>**Код сервера чата: <code>unix_chat_server_c_1.txt**</code></h4><div class="react-renderer node-codeBlock"><pre as="pre" spellcheck="false" class="code-block-wrapper group/codeblock" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div class="absolute top-2 right-2 z-1 flex items-center gap-0.5 transition-opacity select-none opacity-0 group-hover/codeblock:opacity-100" contenteditable="false"><button type="button" class="flex items-center justify-center text-center font-medium cursor-pointer outline-hidden focus-visible:ring-3 xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy size-3.5" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div><code><div data-node-view-content="" style="white-space: pre-wrap;"><div data-node-view-content-react="" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: inherit;"><span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/socket.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/un.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/select.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;stdio.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;stdlib.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;unistd.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;string.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;errno.h&gt;</span>

<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">define</span><span class="hljs-meta"> SOCKET_PATH </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">"/tmp/unix_chat_socket"</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">define</span><span class="hljs-meta"> MAX_CLIENTS 10</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">define</span><span class="hljs-meta"> BUFFER_SIZE 256</span>

<span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">main</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> server_fd, client_fds[MAX_CLIENTS];
    <span class="hljs-class hljs-keyword">struct</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">sockaddr_un</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">server_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">, </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">client_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">;</span>
    fd_set read_fds, master_fds;
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> max_fd = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
    <span class="hljs-type">char</span> buffer[BUFFER_SIZE];
    <span class="hljs-type">ssize_t</span> bytes_read;

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Инициализируем массив дескрипторов клиентов</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (<span class="hljs-type">int</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; MAX_CLIENTS; i++) {
        client_fds[i] = <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>;
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Создаём сокет</span>
    server_fd = socket(AF_UNIX, SOCK_STREAM, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (server_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"socket"</span>);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Удаляем файл сокета, если он уже существует</span>
    unlink(SOCKET_PATH);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Инициализируем адрес сервера</span>
    <span class="hljs-built_in">memset</span>(&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr));
    server_addr.sun_family = AF_UNIX;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">strncpy</span>(server_addr.sun_path, SOCKET_PATH, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr.sun_path) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Связываем сокет с файлом</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bind(server_fd, (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr)) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"bind"</span>);
        close(server_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Переводим сокет в режим прослушивания</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (listen(server_fd, MAX_CLIENTS) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"listen"</span>);
        close(server_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Инициализируем master_fds</span>
    FD_ZERO(&amp;master_fds);
    FD_SET(server_fd, &amp;master_fds);
    max_fd = server_fd;

    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Chat Server: Waiting for connections...\n"</span>);

    <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> (<span class="hljs-number">1</span>) {
        <span class="hljs-comment">// Копируем master_fds в read_fds</span>
        read_fds = master_fds;

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Ждём активности на любом из дескрипторов</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (select(max_fd + <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, &amp;read_fds, <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>, <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>, <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"select"</span>);
            <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Проверяем серверный сокет на новые соединения</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (FD_ISSET(server_fd, &amp;read_fds)) {
            <span class="hljs-type">socklen_t</span> client_len = <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(client_addr);
            <span class="hljs-type">int</span> client_fd = accept(server_fd, (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;client_addr, &amp;client_len);
            <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
                perror(<span class="hljs-string">"accept"</span>);
            } <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
                <span class="hljs-comment">// Добавляем нового клиента в master_fds</span>
                <span class="hljs-type">int</span> i;
                <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; MAX_CLIENTS; i++) {
                    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fds[i] == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
                        client_fds[i] = client_fd;
                        <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
                    }
                }
                <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (i == MAX_CLIENTS) {
                    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Chat Server: Too many clients\n"</span>);
                    close(client_fd);
                } <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
                    FD_SET(client_fd, &amp;master_fds);
                    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fd &gt; max_fd) {
                        max_fd = client_fd;
                    }
                    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Chat Server: New client connected (fd=%d)\n"</span>, client_fd);
                }
            }
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Проверяем клиентские сокеты на данные</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (<span class="hljs-type">int</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; MAX_CLIENTS; i++) {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fds[i] != <span class="hljs-number">-1</span> &amp;&amp; FD_ISSET(client_fds[i], &amp;read_fds)) {
                bytes_read = recv(client_fds[i], buffer, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(buffer) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
                <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bytes_read &lt;= <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
                    <span class="hljs-comment">// Клиент отключился</span>
                    close(client_fds[i]);
                    FD_CLR(client_fds[i], &amp;master_fds);
                    client_fds[i] = <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>;
                    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Chat Server: Client disconnected (fd=%d)\n"</span>, client_fds[i]);
                } <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
                    buffer[bytes_read] = <span class="hljs-string">'\0'</span>;
                    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Chat Server: Received from client %d: %s\n"</span>, client_fds[i], buffer);

                    <span class="hljs-comment">// Рассылаем сообщение всем клиентам</span>
                    <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (<span class="hljs-type">int</span> j = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; j &lt; MAX_CLIENTS; j++) {
                        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fds[j] != <span class="hljs-number">-1</span> &amp;&amp; client_fds[j] != client_fds[i]) {
                            <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (send(client_fds[j], buffer, bytes_read, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
                                perror(<span class="hljs-string">"send"</span>);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Закрываем все сокеты и удаляем файл</span>
    close(server_fd);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (<span class="hljs-type">int</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; MAX_CLIENTS; i++) {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fds[i] != <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
            close(client_fds[i]);
        }
    }
    unlink(SOCKET_PATH);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
}</div></div></code></pre></div><h4>**Код клиента чата: <code>unix_chat_client_c_1.txt**</code></h4><div class="react-renderer node-codeBlock"><pre as="pre" spellcheck="false" class="code-block-wrapper group/codeblock" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div class="absolute top-2 right-2 z-1 flex items-center gap-0.5 transition-opacity select-none class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/socket.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/un.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;stdio.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;stdlib.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;unistd.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;string.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;errno.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;pthread.h&gt;</span>

<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">define</span><span class="hljs-meta"> SOCKET_PATH </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">"/tmp/unix_chat_socket"</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">define</span><span class="hljs-meta"> BUFFER_SIZE 256</span>

<span class="hljs-type">void</span> *<span class="hljs-title function_">receive_thread</span><span class="hljs-params">(</span><span class="hljs-params hljs-type">void</span><span class="hljs-params"> *arg)</span> {
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> client_fd = *(<span class="hljs-type">int</span> *)arg;
    <span class="hljs-type">char</span> buffer[BUFFER_SIZE];
    <span class="hljs-type">ssize_t</span> bytes_read;

    <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> (<span class="hljs-number">1</span>) {
        bytes_read = recv(client_fd, buffer, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(buffer) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bytes_read &lt;= <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
        }
        buffer[bytes_read] = <span class="hljs-string">'\0'</span>;
        <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Received: %s\n"</span>, buffer);
    }

    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>;
}

<span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">main</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> client_fd;
    <span class="hljs-class hljs-keyword">struct</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">sockaddr_un</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">server_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">;</span>
    <span class="hljs-type">pthread_t</span> tid;

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Создаём сокет</span>
    client_fd = socket(AF_UNIX, SOCK_STREAM, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"socket"</span>);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Инициализируем адрес сервера</span>
    <span class="hljs-built_in">memset</span>(&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr));
    server_addr.sun_family = AF_UNIX;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">strncpy</span>(server_addr.sun_path, SOCKET_PATH, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr.sun_path) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Подключаемся к серверу</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (connect(client_fd, (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr)) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"connect"</span>);
        close(client_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Chat Client: Connected to server. Type messages below.\n"</span>);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Запускаем поток для получения сообщений</span>
    pthread_create(&amp;tid, <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>, receive_thread, &amp;client_fd);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Читаем ввод пользователя и отправляем на сервер</span>
    <span class="hljs-type">char</span> input[BUFFER_SIZE];
    <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> (fgets(input, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(input), <span class="hljs-built_in">stdin</span>) != <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>) {
        input[<span class="hljs-built_in">strcspn</span>(input, <span class="hljs-string">"\n"</span>)] = <span class="hljs-string">'\0'</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// Удаляем символ новой строки</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (send(client_fd, input, <span class="hljs-built_in">strlen</span>(input), <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"send"</span>);
            <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
        }
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Закрываем сокет и ждём завершения потока</span>
    close(client_fd);
    pthread_join(tid, <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
}</div></div></code></pre></div><h4><strong>Как запустить чат:</strong></h4><ol><li><p>Скомпилируйте сервер и клиент:</p><div class="react-renderer node-codeBlock"><pre as="pre" spellcheck="false" Передача файлов через Unix Domain Sockets</strong></h3><p>В этом примере клиент отправляет файл серверу, который сохраняет его на диске.</p><h4>**Код сервера для передачи файлов: <code>unix_file_server_c_1.txt**</code></h4><div class="react-renderer node-codeBlock"><pre as="pre" spellcheck="false" class="code-block-wrapper group/codeblock" data-node-view-wrapper=""
