class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/socket.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/un.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;stdio.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;stdlib.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;unistd.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;string.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;errno.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;fcntl.h&gt;</span>

<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">define</span><span class="hljs-meta"> SOCKET_PATH </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">"/tmp/unix_file_socket"</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">define</span><span class="hljs-meta"> BUFFER_SIZE 4096</span>

<span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">main</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> server_fd, client_fd;
    <span class="hljs-class hljs-keyword">struct</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">sockaddr_un</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">server_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">, </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">client_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">;</span>
    <span class="hljs-type">socklen_t</span> client_len;
    <span class="hljs-type">char</span> buffer[BUFFER_SIZE];
    <span class="hljs-type">ssize_t</span> bytes_read;
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> file_fd;
    <span class="hljs-type">char</span> filename[<span class="hljs-number">256</span>];

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Создаём сокет</span>
    server_fd = socket(AF_UNIX, SOCK_STREAM, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (server_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"socket"</span>);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Удаляем файл сокета, если он уже существует</span>
    unlink(SOCKET_PATH);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Инициализируем адрес сервера</span>
    <span class="hljs-built_in">memset</span>(&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr));
    server_addr.sun_family = AF_UNIX;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">strncpy</span>(server_addr.sun_path, SOCKET_PATH, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr.sun_path) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Связываем сокет с файлом</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bind(server_fd, (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr)) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"bind"</span>);
        close(server_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Переводим сокет в режим прослушивания</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (listen(server_fd, <span class="hljs-number">1</span>) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"listen"</span>);
        close(server_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"File Server: Waiting for connections...\n"</span>);

    <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> (<span class="hljs-number">1</span>) {
        <span class="hljs-comment">// Принимаем входящее соединение</span>
        client_len = <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(client_addr);
        client_fd = accept(server_fd, (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;client_addr, &amp;client_len);
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"accept"</span>);
            <span class="hljs-keyword">continue</span>;
        }

        <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"File Server: Client connected\n"</span>);

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Получаем имя файла от клиента</span>
        bytes_read = recv(client_fd, filename, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(filename) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bytes_read &lt;= <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"recv (filename)"</span>);
            close(client_fd);
            <span class="hljs-keyword">continue</span>;
        }
        filename[bytes_read] = <span class="hljs-string">'\0'</span>;
        <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"File Server: Receiving file: %s\n"</span>, filename);

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Создаём файл для записи</span>
        file_fd = open(filename, O_CREAT | O_WRONLY | O_TRUNC, <span class="hljs-number">0666</span>);
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (file_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"open"</span>);
            close(client_fd);
            <span class="hljs-keyword">continue</span>;
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Получаем данные файла от клиента и записываем в файл</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> ((bytes_read = recv(client_fd, buffer, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(buffer), <span class="hljs-number">0</span>)) &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (write(file_fd, buffer, bytes_read) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
                perror(<span class="hljs-string">"write"</span>);
                <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
            }
        }

        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bytes_read == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"recv (file data)"</span>);
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Закрываем файл и соединение с клиентом</span>
        close(file_fd);
        close(client_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"File Server: File received and saved as %s\n"</span>, filename);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Закрываем серверный сокет и удаляем файл</span>
    close(server_fd);
    unlink(SOCKET_PATH);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
}</div></div></code></pre></div><h4>**Код клиента для передачи файлов: <code>unix_file_client_c_1.txt**</code></h4><div class="react-renderer node-codeBlock"><pre as="pre" spellcheck="false" class="code-block-wrapper group/codeblock" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div class="absolute top-2 right-2 z-1 flex items-center gap-0.5 transition-opacity select-none class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/socket.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/un.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;stdio.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;stdlib.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;unistd.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;string.h&gt;</span>

<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">define</span><span class="hljs-meta"> SOCKET_PATH </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">"/tmp/unix_file_socket"</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">define</span><span class="hljs-meta"> BUFFER_SIZE 4096</span>

<span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">main</span><span class="hljs-params">(</span><span class="hljs-params hljs-type">int</span><span class="hljs-params"> argc, </span><span class="hljs-params hljs-type">char</span><span class="hljs-params"> *argv[])</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (argc != <span class="hljs-number">2</span>) {
        <span class="hljs-built_in">fprintf</span>(<span class="hljs-built_in">stderr</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"Usage: %s &lt;filename&gt;\n"</span>, argv[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>]);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> client_fd;
    <span class="hljs-class hljs-keyword">struct</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">sockaddr_un</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">server_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">;</span>
    <span class="hljs-type">char</span> buffer[BUFFER_SIZE];
    <span class="hljs-type">ssize_t</span> bytes_read;
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> file_fd;
    <span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">char</span> *filename = argv[<span class="hljs-number">1</span>];

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Открываем файл для чтения</span>
    file_fd = open(filename, O_RDONLY);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (file_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"open"</span>);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Создаём сокет</span>
    client_fd = socket(AF_UNIX, SOCK_STREAM, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"socket"</span>);
        close(file_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Инициализируем адрес сервера</span>
    <span class="hljs-built_in">memset</span>(&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr));
    server_addr.sun_family = AF_UNIX;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">strncpy</span>(server_addr.sun_path, SOCKET_PATH, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr.sun_path) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Подключаемся к серверу</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (connect(client_fd, (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr)) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"connect"</span>);
        close(file_fd);
        close(client_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"File Client: Connected to server. Sending file: %s\n"</span>, filename);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Отправляем имя файла серверу</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (send(client_fd, filename, <span class="hljs-built_in">strlen</span>(filename), <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"send (filename)"</span>);
        close(file_fd);
        close(client_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Читаем файл и отправляем его серверу</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> ((bytes_read = read(file_fd, buffer, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(buffer))) &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (send(client_fd, buffer, bytes_read, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"send (file data)"</span>);
            <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
        }
    }

    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bytes_read == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"read"</span>);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Закрываем файл и сокет</span>
    close(file_fd);
    close(client_fd);
    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"File Client: File sent successfully\n"</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
}</div></div></code></pre></div><h4><strong>Как запустить передачу файлов:</strong></h4><ol><li><p>Скомпилируйте сервер и клиент:</p><div class="react-renderer node-codeBlock"><pre as="pre" contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>6.3. Реализация RPC (Remote Procedure Call) через Unix Domain Sockets</strong></h3><p>В этом примере клиент вызывает функцию на сервере, как если бы она была локальной.</p><h4>**Код сервера RPC: xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy size-3.5" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div><code><div data-node-view-content="" style="white-space: pre-wrap;"><div data-node-view-content-react="" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: inherit;"><span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/socket.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;sys/un.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;stdio.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;stdlib.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;unistd.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;string.h&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">include</span><span class="hljs-meta"> </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">&lt;errno.h&gt;</span>

<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">define</span><span class="hljs-meta"> SOCKET_PATH </span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-string">"/tmp/unix_rpc_socket"</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">define</span><span class="hljs-meta"> BUFFER_SIZE 256</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// Функция, которую можно вызвать удалённо</span>
<span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">add</span><span class="hljs-params">(</span><span class="hljs-params hljs-type">int</span><span class="hljs-params"> a, </span><span class="hljs-params hljs-type">int</span><span class="hljs-params"> b)</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> a + b;
}

<span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">multiply</span><span class="hljs-params">(</span><span class="hljs-params hljs-type">int</span><span class="hljs-params"> a, </span><span class="hljs-params hljs-type">int</span><span class="hljs-params"> b)</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> a * b;
}

<span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">main</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> server_fd, client_fd;
    <span class="hljs-class hljs-keyword">struct</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">sockaddr_un</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">server_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">, </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">client_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">;</span>
    <span class="hljs-type">socklen_t</span> client_len;
    <span class="hljs-type">char</span> buffer[BUFFER_SIZE];
    <span class="hljs-type">ssize_t</span> bytes_read;
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> a, b, result;
    <span class="hljs-type">char</span> operation;

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Создаём сокет</span>
    server_fd = socket(AF_UNIX, SOCK_STREAM, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (server_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"socket"</span>);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Удаляем файл сокета, если он уже существует</span>
    unlink(SOCKET_PATH);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Инициализируем адрес сервера</span>
    <span class="hljs-built_in">memset</span>(&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr));
    server_addr.sun_family = AF_UNIX;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">strncpy</span>(server_addr.sun_path, SOCKET_PATH, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr.sun_path) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Связываем сокет с файлом</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bind(server_fd, (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr)) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"bind"</span>);
        close(server_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Переводим сокет в режим прослушивания</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (listen(server_fd, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"listen"</span>);
        close(server_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"RPC Server: Waiting for connections...\n"</span>);

    <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> (<span class="hljs-number">1</span>) {
        <span class="hljs-comment">// Принимаем входящее соединение</span>
        client_len = <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(client_addr);
        client_fd = accept(server_fd, (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;client_addr, &amp;client_len);
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"accept"</span>);
            <span class="hljs-keyword">continue</span>;
        }

        <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"RPC Server: Client connected\n"</span>);

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Читаем запрос от клиента (формат: "операция a b")</span>
        bytes_read = recv(client_fd, buffer, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(buffer) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bytes_read &lt;= <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"recv"</span>);
            close(client_fd);
            <span class="hljs-keyword">continue</span>;
        }
        buffer[bytes_read] = <span class="hljs-string">'\0'</span>;

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Разбираем запрос</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (<span class="hljs-built_in">sscanf</span>(buffer, <span class="hljs-string">"%c %d %d"</span>, &amp;operation, &amp;a, &amp;b) != <span class="hljs-number">3</span>) {
            <span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">char</span> *error = <span class="hljs-string">"Invalid request format. Use: &lt;op&gt; &lt;a&gt; &lt;b&gt;"</span>;
            send(client_fd, error, <span class="hljs-built_in">strlen</span>(error), <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
            close(client_fd);
            <span class="hljs-keyword">continue</span>;
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Выполняем операцию</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">switch</span> (operation) {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-string">'+'</span>:
                result = add(a, b);
                <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
            <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-string">'*'</span>:
                result = multiply(a, b);
                <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
            <span class="hljs-keyword">default</span>:
                <span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">char</span> *error = <span class="hljs-string">"Unsupported operation. Use + or *"</span>;
                send(client_fd, error, <span class="hljs-built_in">strlen</span>(error), <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
                close(client_fd);
                <span class="hljs-keyword">continue</span>;
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Отправляем результат клиенту</span>
        <span class="hljs-built_in">sprintf</span>(buffer, <span class="hljs-string">"Result: %d"</span>, result);
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (send(client_fd, buffer, <span class="hljs-built_in">strlen</span>(buffer), <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"send"</span>);
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Закрываем соединение с клиентом</span>
        close(client_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"RPC Server: Request processed: %c %d %d = %d\n"</span>, operation, a, b, result);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Закрываем серверный сокет и удаляем файл</span>
    close(server_fd);
    unlink(SOCKET_PATH);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
}</div></div></code></pre></div><h4>**Код клиента RPC: <code>unix_rpc_client_c_1.txt**</code></h4><div class="react-renderer node-codeBlock"><pre as="pre" spellcheck="false" class="code-block-wrapper <span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">main</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> client_fd;
    <span class="hljs-class hljs-keyword">struct</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">sockaddr_un</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">server_addr</span><span class="hljs-class">;</span>
    <span class="hljs-type">char</span> buffer[BUFFER_SIZE];
    <span class="hljs-type">ssize_t</span> bytes_read;
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> a, b;
    <span class="hljs-type">char</span> operation;

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Создаём сокет</span>
    client_fd = socket(AF_UNIX, SOCK_STREAM, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"socket"</span>);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Инициализируем адрес сервера</span>
    <span class="hljs-built_in">memset</span>(&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr));
    server_addr.sun_family = AF_UNIX;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">strncpy</span>(server_addr.sun_path, SOCKET_PATH, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr.sun_path) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Подключаемся к серверу</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (connect(client_fd, (<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> sockaddr *)&amp;server_addr, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(server_addr)) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"connect"</span>);
        close(client_fd);
        <span class="hljs-built_in">exit</span>(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"RPC Client: Connected to server. Enter operation (e.g., + 5 3):\n"</span>);

    <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> (<span class="hljs-number">1</span>) {
        <span class="hljs-comment">// Читаем ввод пользователя</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (fgets(buffer, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(buffer), <span class="hljs-built_in">stdin</span>) == <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>) {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Удаляем символ новой строки</span>
        buffer[<span class="hljs-built_in">strcspn</span>(buffer, <span class="hljs-string">"\n"</span>)] = <span class="hljs-string">'\0'</span>;

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Отправляем запрос серверу</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (send(client_fd, buffer, <span class="hljs-built_in">strlen</span>(buffer), <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"send"</span>);
            <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// Получаем ответ от сервера</span>
        bytes_read = recv(client_fd, buffer, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(buffer) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bytes_read &lt;= <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
            perror(<span class="hljs-string">"recv"</span>);
            <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
        }

        buffer[bytes_read] = <span class="hljs-string">'\0'</span>;
        <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"RPC Client: %s\n"</span>, buffer);
    }

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Закрываем сокет</span>
    close(client_fd);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
}</div></div></code></pre></div><h4><strong>Как запустить RPC:</strong></h4><ol><li><p>Скомпилируйте сервер и клиент:</p><div class="react-renderer node-codeBlock"><pre as="pre" spellcheck="false" aria-disabled:cursor-not-allowed aria-busy:cursor-wait aria-busy:text-transparent aria-disabled:aria-busy:text-transparent bg-state-ghost text-default hover:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-hover xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide <span class="hljs-built_in">memset</span>(&amp;addr, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(addr));
addr.sun_family = AF_UNIX;
<span class="hljs-built_in">strncpy</span>(addr.sun_path, <span class="hljs-string">"/tmp/my_socket"</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(addr.sun_path) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>);</div></div></code></pre></div></li><li><p>Проверяйте возвращаемые значения функций (<code>socket</code>, <code>bind</code>, <code>connect</code> и т. д.).</p></li></ul><hr contenteditable="false"><h3>**7.7. Блокировка на <code>accept()</code> или <code>recv()**</code></h3><p><strong>Проблема:</strong><br>Программа зависает на <code>accept()</code> или <code>recv()</code>.</p><p><strong>Причина:</strong></p><ul><li><p>Сервер ожидает соединение, но клиент не подключается.</p></li><li><p>Клиент ожидает данные, но сервер не отправляет их.</p></li></ul><p><strong>Решение:</strong></p><ul><li><p>Используйте <strong>неблокирующий режим</strong> (<code>fcntl</code> с <code>O_NONBLOCK</code>):</p><div class="react-renderer node-codeBlock"><pre as="pre" spellcheck="false" class="code-block-wrapper group/codeblock" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div class="absolute top-2 right-2 z-1 flex items-center gap-0.5 transition-opacity select-none opacity-0 group-hover/codeblock:opacity-100" contenteditable="false"><button type="button" class="flex items-center justify-center text-center font-medium cursor-pointer outline-hidden focus-visible:ring-3 relative whitespace-nowrap transition-colors focus-visible:ring-default focus-visible:ring-offset-1 aria-disabled:text-hint aria-disabled:cursor-not-allowed aria-busy:cursor-wait aria-busy:text-transparent aria-disabled:aria-busy:text-transparent bg-state-ghost text-default hover:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-hover active:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-press h-6 gap-1 px-1.5 text-xs rounded-md" aria-haspopup="dialog" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="radix-_r_me_" data-state="closed">C<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down ms-1 size-3 opacity-50" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button><button type="button" class="flex items-center justify-center text-center font-medium cursor-pointer outline-hidden focus-visible:ring-3 relative whitespace-nowrap transition-colors focus-visible:ring-default focus-visible:ring-offset-1 aria-disabled:text-hint aria-disabled:cursor-not-allowed aria-busy:cursor-wait aria-busy:text-transparent aria-disabled:aria-busy:text-transparent bg-state-ghost text-default hover:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-hover active:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-press gap-1 text-xs p-0 rounded-md size-6"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy size-3.5" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div><code><div data-node-view-content="" style="white-space: pre-wrap;"><div data-node-view-content-react="" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: inherit;"><span class="hljs-type">int</span> flags = fcntl(server_fd, F_GETFL, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
fcntl(server_fd, F_SETFL, flags | O_NONBLOCK);</div></div></code></pre></div></li><li><p>Используйте <code>select()</code> или <code>poll()</code> для мультиплексирования:</p><div class="react-renderer node-codeBlock"><pre as="pre" spellcheck="false" class="code-block-wrapper group/codeblock" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div class="absolute top-2 right-2 z-1 flex items-center gap-0.5 transition-opacity select-none opacity-0 group-hover/codeblock:opacity-100" contenteditable="false"><button type="button" class="flex items-center justify-center aria-disabled:cursor-not-allowed aria-busy:cursor-wait aria-busy:text-transparent aria-disabled:aria-busy:text-transparent bg-state-ghost text-default hover:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-hover active:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-press h-6 gap-1 px-1.5 text-xs rounded-md" aria-haspopup="dialog" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="radix-_r_kf_" data-state="closed">C<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down ms-1 size-3 opacity-50" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button><button type="button" class="flex items-center justify-center text-center font-medium Оптимизация и лучшие практики</strong></h2><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>8.1. Используйте <code>select()</code> или <code>poll()</code> для обработки нескольких клиентов</strong></h3><p>Для обработки нескольких клиентов одновременно используйте <code>select()</code> или <code>poll()</code> для мультиплексирования ввода-вывода.</p><h4><strong>Пример с <code>select()</code>:</strong></h4><div class="react-renderer node-codeBlock"><pre as="pre" spellcheck="false" class="code-block-wrapper group/codeblock" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div class="absolute top-2 right-2 z-1 flex items-center gap-0.5 transition-opacity select-none opacity-0 group-hover/codeblock:opacity-100" contenteditable="false"><button type="button" class="flex items-center justify-center text-center font-medium cursor-pointer outline-hidden focus-visible:ring-3 relative whitespace-nowrap transition-colors focus-visible:ring-default focus-visible:ring-offset-1 aria-disabled:text-hint aria-disabled:cursor-not-allowed aria-busy:cursor-wait aria-busy:text-transparent aria-disabled:aria-busy:text-transparent bg-state-ghost text-default hover:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-hover active:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-press h-6 gap-1 px-1.5 text-xs rounded-md" aria-haspopup="dialog" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="radix-_r_l8_" data-state="closed">C<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down ms-1 size-3 opacity-50" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button><button type="button" class="flex items-center justify-center text-center font-medium cursor-pointer outline-hidden focus-visible:ring-3 relative whitespace-nowrap transition-colors focus-visible:ring-default focus-visible:ring-offset-1 aria-disabled:text-hint aria-disabled:cursor-not-allowed aria-busy:cursor-wait aria-busy:text-transparent aria-disabled:aria-busy:text-transparent bg-state-ghost text-default hover:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-hover active:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-press gap-1 text-xs p-0 rounded-md size-6"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy size-3.5" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div><code><div data-node-view-content="" style="white-space: pre-wrap;"><div data-node-view-content-react="" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: inherit;">fd_set read_fds, master_fds;
FD_ZERO(&amp;master_fds);
FD_SET(server_fd, &amp;master_fds);
<span class="hljs-type">int</span> max_fd = server_fd;

<span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> (<span class="hljs-number">1</span>) {
    read_fds = master_fds;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (select(max_fd + <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, &amp;read_fds, <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>, <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>, <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>) == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"select"</span>);
        <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
    }

    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (FD_ISSET(server_fd, &amp;read_fds)) {
        <span class="hljs-comment">// Новое соединение</span>
        <span class="hljs-type">int</span> client_fd = accept(server_fd, <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>, <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>);
        FD_SET(client_fd, &amp;master_fds);
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fd &gt; max_fd) {
            max_fd = client_fd;
        }
    }

    <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (<span class="hljs-type">int</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt;= max_fd; i++) {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (FD_ISSET(i, &amp;read_fds) &amp;&amp; i != server_fd) {
            <span class="hljs-comment">// Данные от клиента</span>
            <span class="hljs-type">char</span> buffer[<span class="hljs-number">256</span>];
            <span class="hljs-type">ssize_t</span> bytes_read = recv(i, buffer, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(buffer), <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
            <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bytes_read &lt;= <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
                close(i);
                FD_CLR(i, &amp;master_fds);
            } <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
                <span class="hljs-comment">// Обрабатываем данные</span>
            }
        }
    }
}</div></div></code></pre></div><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>8.2. Используйте неблокирующий режим для высокопроизводительных приложений</strong></h3><p>Если ваше приложение должно обрабатывать <strong>много запросов</strong> без блокировки, используйте неблокирующий режим.</p><h4><strong>Пример:</strong></h4><div class="react-renderer node-codeBlock"><pre as="pre" spellcheck="false" class="code-block-wrapper group/codeblock" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div class="absolute top-2 right-2 z-1 flex items-center gap-0.5 transition-opacity select-none opacity-0 group-hover/codeblock:opacity-100" contenteditable="false"><button type="button" class="flex items-center justify-center text-center font-medium cursor-pointer outline-hidden focus-visible:ring-3 relative whitespace-nowrap aria-disabled:aria-busy:text-transparent bg-state-ghost text-default hover:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-hover active:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-press h-6 gap-1 px-1.5 text-xs rounded-md" aria-haspopup="dialog" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="radix-_r_li_" data-state="closed">C<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" aria-disabled:aria-busy:text-transparent bg-state-ghost text-default hover:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-hover active:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-press gap-1 text-xs p-0 rounded-md size-6"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy size-3.5" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div><code><div data-node-view-content="" style="white-space: pre-wrap;"><div data-node-view-content-react="" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: inherit;"><span class="hljs-type">int</span> flags = fcntl(server_fd, F_GETFL, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
fcntl(server_fd, F_SETFL, flags | O_NONBLOCK);

<span class="hljs-type">int</span> client_fd = accept(server_fd, <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>, <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>);
<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (client_fd == <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (errno == EAGAIN || errno == EWOULDBLOCK) {
        <span class="hljs-comment">// Нет новых соединений</span>
    } <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
        perror(<span class="hljs-string">"accept"</span>);
    }
}</div></div></code></pre></div><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>8.3. Устанавливайте таймауты для операций</strong></h3><p>Используйте <code>setsockopt()</code> для установки таймаутов на операции <code>recv()</code> и <code>send()</code>.</p><h4><strong>Пример:</strong></h4><div class="react-renderer node-codeBlock"><pre as="pre" spellcheck="false" class="code-block-wrapper group/codeblock" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div class="absolute top-2 right-2 z-1 flex items-center gap-0.5 transition-opacity select-none opacity-0 group-hover/codeblock:opacity-100" contenteditable="false"><button type="button" class="flex items-center justify-center text-center font-medium cursor-pointer outline-hidden focus-visible:ring-3 relative whitespace-nowrap transition-colors focus-visible:ring-default focus-visible:ring-offset-1 aria-disabled:text-hint aria-disabled:cursor-not-allowed aria-busy:cursor-wait aria-busy:text-transparent aria-haspopup="dialog" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="radix-_r_l5_" data-state="closed">C<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" 6-6"></path></svg></button><button type="button" class="flex items-center justify-center text-center font-medium cursor-pointer outline-hidden focus-visible:ring-3 relative whitespace-nowrap aria-disabled:aria-busy:text-transparent bg-state-ghost text-default hover:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-hover active:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-press gap-1 text-xs p-0 rounded-md size-6"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy size-3.5" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div><code><div data-node-view-content="" style="white-space: pre-wrap;"><div data-node-view-content-react="" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: inherit;"><span class="hljs-class hljs-keyword">struct</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">timeval</span><span class="hljs-class"> </span><span class="hljs-class hljs-title">timeout</span><span class="hljs-class">;</span>
timeout.tv_sec = <span class="hljs-number">5</span>;  <span class="hljs-comment">// 5 секунд</span>
timeout.tv_usec = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;

setsockopt(server_fd, SOL_SOCKET, SO_RCVTIMEO, &amp;timeout, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(timeout));
setsockopt(server_fd, SOL_SOCKET, SO_SNDTIMEO, &amp;timeout, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(timeout));</div></div></code></pre></div><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>8.4. already in use".</p><h4><strong>Пример:</strong></h4><div class="react-renderer node-codeBlock"><pre as="pre" spellcheck="false" class="code-block-wrapper group/codeblock" data-node-view-wrapper="" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide class="hljs-meta">#</span><span class="hljs-meta hljs-keyword">define</span><span class="hljs-meta"> BUFFER_SIZE 4096</span>
<span class="hljs-type">char</span> buffer[BUFFER_SIZE];
<span class="hljs-type">ssize_t</span> bytes_read;

<span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> ((bytes_read = recv(client_fd, buffer, BUFFER_SIZE, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>)) &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
    <span class="hljs-comment">// Обрабатываем данные в буфере</span>

as="pre" spellcheck="false" class="code-block-wrapper group/codeblock" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div class="absolute top-2 right-2 z-1 flex items-center gap-0.5 d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button><button type="button" class="flex items-center justify-center text-center font-medium cursor-pointer outline-hidden focus-visible:ring-3 relative whitespace-nowrap transition-colors focus-visible:ring-default focus-visible:ring-offset-1 aria-disabled:text-hint aria-disabled:cursor-not-allowed aria-busy:cursor-wait aria-busy:text-transparent aria-disabled:aria-busy:text-transparent bg-state-ghost text-default hover:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-hover active:not-disabled:bg-state-ghost-press gap-1 text-xs p-0 rounded-md size-6"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy size-3.5" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button></div><code><div data-node-view-content="" style="white-space: pre-wrap;"><div data-node-view-content-react="" data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: inherit;"><span class="hljs-type">char</span> buffer[<span class="hljs-number">256</span>];
<span class="hljs-type">ssize_t</span> bytes_read = recv(client_fd, buffer, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(buffer) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (bytes_read &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
    buffer[bytes_read] = <span class="hljs-string">'\0'</span>;  <span class="hljs-comment">// Добавляем завершающий нуль</span>
    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Received: %s\n"</span>, buffer);
}</div></div></code></pre></div><hr contenteditable="false"><hr contenteditable="false"><h2><strong>9. Сравнение с другими механизмами IPC</strong></h2><table style="min-width: 150px"><colgroup><col style="min-width: 25px"><col style="min-width: 25px"><col style="min-width: 25px"><col style="min-width: 25px"><col style="min-width: 25px"><col style="min-width: 25px"></colgroup><tbody><tr><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Механизм IPC</strong></p></th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Unix Domain Sockets</strong></p></th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Разделяемая память</strong></p></th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Очереди сообщений</strong></p></th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Каналы (Pipe/FIFO)</strong></p></th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Сетевые сокеты (AF_INET)</strong></p></th></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Скорость</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>⭐⭐⭐⭐ (очень высокая)</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐ (максимальная)</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>⭐⭐⭐ (средняя)</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>⭐⭐ (низкая)</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>⭐⭐ (низкая)</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Тип обмена</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Потоковый/датаграммный</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Память</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Сообщения</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Поток байтов</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Поток байтов</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Локальность</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Локальные (одна машина)</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Локальные</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Локальные</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Локальные</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Сетевые (между машинами)</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Синхронизация</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Требуется вручную</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Требуется вручную</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Встроенная</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Нет</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Требуется вручную</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Поддержка структур</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Да (сериализация)</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Да (прямой доступ)</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Да (сообщения)</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Нет</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Да (сериализация)</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Безопасность</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Права файловой системы</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Права файловой системы</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Права доступа</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Права файловой системы</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Сетевая безопасность</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Сложность</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Средняя</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Высокая</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Низкая</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Низкая</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Средняя</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Переносимость</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Unix-подобные системы</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Unix-подобные системы</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Unix-подобные системы</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>POSIX</p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Все системы</p></td></tr></tbody></table><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>Когда использовать Unix Domain Sockets?</strong></h3><p>✅ <strong>Используйте Unix Domain Sockets, если:</strong></p><ul><li><p>Вам нужен <strong>быстрый обмен данными между процессами на одной машине</strong>.</p></li><li><p>Вы хотите использовать <strong>знакомый API сокетов</strong> (аналогично сетевым сокетам).</p></li><li><p>Вам нужна <strong>поддержка потокового (SOCK_STREAM) или датаграммного (SOCK_DGRAM) обмена</strong>.</p></li><li><p>Вы хотите <strong>изолировать процессы</strong> (например, для микросервисов или модулей программы).</p></li><li><p>Вам нужна <strong>поддержка протоколов типа RPC</strong> (вызов удалённых процедур).</p></li></ul><p>❌ <strong>Не используйте Unix Domain Sockets, если:</strong></p><ul><li><p>Вам нужен <strong>обмен данными между разными машинами</strong> (используйте сетевые сокеты <code>AF_INET</code>).</p></li><li><p>Вам нужна <strong>максимальная производительность</strong> (используйте разделяемую память).</p></li><li><p>Вы передаёте <strong>очень большие объёмы данных</strong> (UDS имеют ограничения на размер сообщений).</p></li></ul><hr contenteditable="false"><hr contenteditable="false"><h2><strong>10. Заключение</strong></h2><p><strong>Unix Domain Sockets (AF_UNIX)</strong> — это <strong>мощный и гибкий</strong> механизм межпроцессового взаимодействия, который позволяет процессам обмениваться данными <strong>без использования сетевого стека</strong>. Они идеально подходят для <strong>локального обмена данными</strong> между процессами на одной машине и предоставляют <strong>знакомый API</strong>, аналогичный сетевым сокетам.</p><h3><strong>Краткое резюме:</strong></h3><table style="min-width: 50px"><colgroup><col style="min-width: 25px"><col style="min-width: 25px"></colgroup><tbody><tr><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Аспект</strong></p></th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Описание</strong></p></th></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Тип сокета</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>AF_UNIX</code> (семейство адресов).</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Типы обмена</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><code>SOCK_STREAM</code> (потоковый), <code>SOCK_DGRAM</code> (датаграммный), <code>SOCK_SEQPACKET</code> (последовательный пакетный).</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Идентификация</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Файл в файловой системе (например, <code>/tmp/my_socket</code>).</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Скорость</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Очень высокая (нет оверхеда на сетевой стек).</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Синхронизация</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Требуется вручную (используйте <code>select()</code>, <code>poll()</code> или потоки).</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Безопасность</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Права доступа определяются правами на файл сокета.</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p><strong>Переносимость</strong></p></td><td colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p>Поддерживаются во всех Unix-подобных системах.</p></td></tr></tbody></table><h3><strong>Рекомендации:</strong></h3><p>✅ <strong>Используйте Unix Domain Sockets, если:</strong></p><ul><li><p>Вам нужен <strong>быстрый локальный обмен данными</strong> между процессами.</p></li><li><p>Вы хотите использовать <strong>знакомый API сокетов</strong>.</p></li><li><p>Вам нужна <strong>поддержка потокового или датаграммного обмена</strong>.</p></li></ul><p>✅ <strong>Следуйте лучшим практикам:</strong></p><ul><li><p>Всегда <strong>проверяйте ошибки</strong> при работе с сокетами.</p></li><li><p><strong>Удаляйте файлы сокетов</strong> после использования (<code>unlink()</code>).</p></li><li><p>Используйте <code>**select()</code>/<code>poll()**</code> для обработки нескольких клиентов.</p></li><li><p>Устанавливайте <strong>таймауты</strong> для операций <code>recv()</code>/<code>send()</code>.</p></li><li><p>Избегайте <strong>длительных операций</strong> в критической секции.</p></li></ul><hr contenteditable="false"><hr contenteditable="false"><h2><strong>11. Ссылки и дополнительные ресурсы</strong></h2><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>Мануалы Linux:</strong></h3><ul><li><p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://man7.org/linux/man-pages/man7/unix.7.html">unix(7) — Обзор Unix Domain Sockets</a></p></li><li><p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://man7.org/linux/man-pages/man2/socket.2.html">socket(2) — Создание сокета</a></p></li><li><p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://man7.org/linux/man-pages/man2/bind.2.html">bind(2) — Связывание сокета с адресом</a></p></li><li><p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://man7.org/linux/man-pages/man2/listen.2.html">listen(2) — Перевод сокета в режим прослушивания</a></p></li><li><p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://man7.org/linux/man-pages/man2/accept.2.html">accept(2) — Принятие соединения</a></p></li><li><p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://man7.org/linux/man-pages/man2/connect.2.html">connect(2) — Подключение к сокету</a></p></li><li><p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://man7.org/linux/man-pages/man2/send.2.html">send(2) — Отправка данных</a></p></li><li><p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://man7.org/linux/man-pages/man2/recv.2.html">recv(2) — Получение данных</a></p></li><li><p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://man7.org/linux/man-pages/man2/select.2.html">select(2) — Мультиплексирование ввода-вывода</a></p></li></ul><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>Книги:</strong></h3><ul><li><p><strong>"Linux System Programming"</strong> (Robert Love) — Глава 7: Sockets.</p></li><li><p><strong>"The Linux Programming Interface"</strong> (Michael Kerrisk) — Глава 57: Unix Domain Sockets.</p></li><li><p><strong>"UNIX Network Programming"</strong> (W. Richard Stevens) — Глава 15: Unix Domain Sockets.</p></li></ul><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>Статьи:</strong></h3><ul><li><p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://www.softprayog.in/programming/unix-domain-sockets-in-linux">Unix Domain Sockets in Linux</a></p></li><li><p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://www.baeldung.com/linux/unix-domain-sockets-vs-tcp-ip-sockets">Unix Domain Sockets vs TCP/IP Sockets</a></p></li><li><p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/unix-domain-socket/">Using Unix Domain Sockets for IPC</a></p></li></ul><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>Практические упражнения:</strong></h3><ol><li><p>Реализуйте <strong>простой эхо-сервер</strong> на Unix Domain Sockets, который возвращает клиенту полученное сообщение.</p></li><li><p>Напишите <strong>клиент и сервер</strong>, которые обмениваются <strong>структурированными данными</strong> (например, JSON).</p></li><li><p>Создайте <strong>систему логгирования</strong>, где несколько процессов отправляют логи на сервер через Unix Domain Sockets.</p></li><li><p>Реализуйте <strong>простой RPC-сервер</strong>, который выполняет арифметические операции по запросам клиентов.</p></li><li><p>Сравните <strong>производительность</strong> Unix Domain Sockets и сетевых сокетов (<code>AF_INET</code>) в вашей системе.</p></li></ol><hr contenteditable="false"><hr contenteditable="false"><h2><strong>Приложение: Лимиты и ограничения Unix Domain Sockets</strong></h2><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>Ограничения на путь к сокету</strong></h3><ul><li><p>Максимальная длина пути для <code>sockaddr_un.sun_path</code> — <strong>108 байт</strong> (включая завершающий <code>\0</code>).</p></li><li><p>Обычно пути к сокетам размещают в <code>/tmp/</code> или <code>/var/run/</code>.</p></li></ul><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>Ограничения на размер сообщений</strong></h3><ul><li><p>Размер сообщений для <code>SOCK_DGRAM</code> ограничен <strong>максимальным размером датаграммы</strong> (зависит от реализации ядра, обычно <strong>2-8 КБ</strong>).</p></li><li><p>Для <code>SOCK_STREAM</code> ограничений на размер сообщений нет (данные передаются потоком).</p></li></ul><hr contenteditable="false"><h3><strong>Просмотр активных Unix Domain Sockets</strong></h3><p>Просмотреть активные Unix
